<div class="ng-scope" ng-controller="GettingStartedPageCtrl" style="height: 1100px">\n      <div class="portal-contact-content">\n       <h1 style="margin:0">\n        Getting Started\n       </h1>\n       <div style="float: left; width:500px">\n        <div style="margin-top: 20px">\n         <p>\n          <strong>\n           Steps for getting started (example on right):\n          </strong>\n         </p>\n         <ol>\n          <li>\n           Add references to\n           <a href="http://code.jquery.com/">\n            jQuery\n           </a>\n           and\n           <a href="http://ajax.googleapis.com/ajax/libs/angularjs/1.0.4/angular.min.js">\n            AngularJS\n           </a>\n           .\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Add references to\n           <a href="https://github.com/angular-ui/ng-grid">\n            ngGrid\n           </a>\n           \'s javascript and css files.\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Where you declare your app module, add ngGrid:\n           <br/>\n           <code>\n            angular.module(\'myApp\',[\'ngGrid\']);\n           </code>\n           <br/>\n           If you use\n           <a href="https://github.com/angular/angular-seed" target="blank">\n            angular seed\n           </a>\n           , it is in your app.js file.\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           In your html file within the controller where you plan to use ng-grid, add:\n           <br/>\n           <code>\n            &lt;div class="gridStyle" ng-grid="gridOptions"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;\n           </code>\n           <br/>\n           gridOptions is the variable we are going to bind to where we will initialize our grid options.\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           We are going to define a basic style for our grid in style.css:\n           <pre class="prettyprint" style="margin-top:10px"><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">gridStyle </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">\n    border</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">1px</span><span class="pln"> solid rgb</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="lit">212</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="lit">212</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="lit">212</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">\n    width</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">400px</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln"> \n    height</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">300px</span><span class="pln">\n</span><span class="pun">}</span></pre>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           In your javascript file within the controller where you plan to use\n           <br/>\n           ng-grid, lets add data that our grid will use:\n           <br/>\n          </li>\n          <pre class="prettyprint" style="margin-top:10px"><span class="pln">$scope</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">myData </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">[{</span><span class="pln">name</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">"Moroni"</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> age</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">50</span><span class="pun">},</span><span class="pln">\n                 </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">name</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">"Tiancum"</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> age</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">43</span><span class="pun">},</span><span class="pln">\n                 </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">name</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">"Jacob"</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> age</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">27</span><span class="pun">},</span><span class="pln">\n                 </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">name</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">"Nephi"</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> age</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">29</span><span class="pun">},</span><span class="pln">\n                 </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">name</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">"Enos"</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> age</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">34</span><span class="pun">}];</span></pre>\n          <li>\n           Now initialize your grid options under the same controller as data:\n           <br/>\n           <code>\n            $scope.gridOptions = { data: \'myData\' };\n           </code>\n          </li>\n          <li style="margin-top: 20px">\n           <strong>\n            Below is the outcome of the grid using the example on the right:\n           </strong>\n           <br/>\n          </li>\n         </ol>\n        </div>\n        <div class="ng-scope ngGrid ng1492311715854 unselectable" ng-grid="gridOptions" style="border: 1px solid rgb(212,212,212); width: 400px; height: 300px; margin-left: 25px; margin-top: 20px; ">\n         <div class="ngTopPanel ng-scope" ng-class="{\'ui-widget-header\':jqueryUITheme, \'ui-corner-top\': jqueryUITheme}" ng-style="topPanelStyle()" style="width: 400px; height: 30px;">\n          <div class="ngGroupPanel" ng-show="showGroupPanel()" ng-style="groupPanelStyle()" style="display: none; width: 400px; height: 32px;">\n           <div class="ngGroupPanelDescription ng-binding" ng-show="configGroups.length == 0">\n            Drag a column header here and drop it to group by that column.\n           </div>\n           <ul class="ngGroupList" ng-show="configGroups.length &gt; 0" style="display: none;">\n            <!-- ngRepeat: group in configGroups -->\n           </ul>\n          </div>\n          <div class="ngHeaderContainer" ng-style="headerStyle()" style="width: 400px; height: 30px;">\n           <div class="ngHeaderScroller" ng-header-row="" ng-style="headerScrollerStyle()" style="height: 30px;">\n            <!-- ngRepeat: col in renderedColumns -->\n            <div class="ngHeaderCell ng-scope col0 colt0" ng-class="col.colIndex()" ng-repeat="col in renderedColumns" ng-style="{ height: col.headerRowHeight }" style="height: 30px;">\n             <div class="ngVerticalBar ngVerticalBarVisible" ng-class="{ ngVerticalBarVisible: !$last }" ng-style="{height: col.headerRowHeight}" style="height: 30px;">\n             </div>\n             <div <div class="ng-scope" ng-controller="GettingStartedPageCtrl" style="height: 1100px">\n      <div class="portal-contact-content">\n       <h1 style="margin:0">\n        Getting Started\n       </h1>\n       <div style="float: left; width:500px">\n        <div style="margin-top: 20px">\n         <p>\n          <strong>\n           Steps for getting started (example on right):\n          </strong>\n         </p>\n         <ol>\n          <li>\n           Add references to\n           <a href="http://code.jquery.com/">\n            jQuery\n           </a>\n           and\n           <a href="http://ajax.googleapis.com/ajax/libs/angularjs/1.0.4/angular.min.js">\n            AngularJS\n           </a>\n           .\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Add references to\n           <a href="https://github.com/angular-ui/ng-grid">\n            ngGrid\n           </a>\n           \'s javascript and css files.\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Where you declare your app module, add ngGrid:\n           <br/>\n           <code>\n            angular.module(\'myApp\',[\'ngGrid\']);\n           </code>\n           <br/>\n           If you use\n           <a href="https://github.com/angular/angular-seed" target="blank">\n            angular seed\n           </a>\n           , it is in your app.js file.\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           In your html file within the controller where you plan to use ng-grid, add:\n           <br/>\n           <code>\n            &lt;div class="gridStyle" ng-grid="gridOptions"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;\n           </code>\n           <br/>\n           gridOptions is the variable we are going to bind to where we will initialize our grid options.\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           We are going to define a basic style for our grid in style.css:\n           <pre class="prettyprint" style="margin-top:10px"><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">gridStyle </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">\n    border</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">1px</span><span class="pln"> solid rgb</span><span class="pun">(</span><span class="lit">212</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="lit">212</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="lit">212</span><span class="pun">);</span><span class="pln">\n    width</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">400px</span><span class="pun">;</span><span class="pln"> \n    height</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">300px</span><span class="pln">\n</span><span class="pun">}</span></pre>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           In your javascript file within the controller where you plan to use\n           <br/>\n           ng-grid, lets add data that our grid will use:\n           <br/>\n          </li>\n          <pre class="prettyprint" style="margin-top:10px"><span class="pln">$scope</span><span class="pun">.</span><span class="pln">myData </span><span class="pun">=</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="pun">[{</span><span class="pln">name</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">"Moroni"</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> age</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">50</span><span class="pun">},</span><span class="pln">\n                 </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">name</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">"Tiancum"</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> age</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">43</span><span class="pun">},</span><span class="pln">\n                 </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">name</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">"Jacob"</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> age</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">27</span><span class="pun">},</span><span class="pln">\n                 </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">name</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">"Nephi"</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> age</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">29</span><span class="pun">},</span><span class="pln">\n                 </span><span class="pun">{</span><span class="pln">name</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="str">"Enos"</span><span class="pun">,</span><span class="pln"> age</span><span class="pun">:</span><span class="pln"> </span><span class="lit">34</span><span class="pun">}];</span></pre>\n          <li>\n           Now initialize your grid options under the same controller as data:\n           <br/>\n           <code>\n            $scope.gridOptions = { data: \'myData\' };\n           </code>\n          </li>\n          <li style="margin-top: 20px">\n           <strong>\n            Below is the outcome of the grid using the example on the right:\n           </strong>\n           <br/>\n          </li>\n         </ol>\n        </div>\n        <div class="ng-scope ngGrid ng1492569905372 unselectable" ng-grid="gridOptions" style="border: 1px solid rgb(212,212,212); width: 400px; height: 300px; margin-left: 25px; margin-top: 20px; ">\n         <div class="ngTopPanel ng-scope" ng-class="{\'ui-widget-header\':jqueryUITheme, \'ui-corner-top\': jqueryUITheme}" ng-style="topPanelStyle()" style="width: 400px; height: 30px;">\n          <div     </div>\n             </div>\n            </div>\n            <div class="ngHeaderCell ng-scope col1 colt1" ng-class="col.colIndex()" ng-repeat="col in renderedColumns" ng-style="{ height: col.headerRowHeight }" style="height: 30px;">\n             <div class="ngVerticalBar" ng-class="{ ngVerticalBarVisible: !$last }" ng-style="{height: col.headerRowHeight}" style="height: 30px;">\n             </div>\n             <div ng-header-cell="">\n              <div class="ngHeaderSortColumn " draggable="true" ng-class="{ \'ngSorted\': !col.noSortVisible() }" ng-style="{\'cursor\':   </div>\n               <div class="ngUnPinnedIcon" ng-class="{ ngPinnedIcon: col.pinned, ngUnPinnedIcon: !col.pinned }" ng-click="togglePin(col)" ng-show="col.pinnable" style="display: none;">\n               </div>\n              </div>\n              <div class="ngHeaderGrip ng-scope" ng-click="col.gripClick($event)" ng-mousedown="col.gripOnMouseDown($event)" ng-show="col.resizable"
